function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

if (!is_file('dev/logtest')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/logtest');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('dev/logtest')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/logtest');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/logtest') != 'b081c91eca8e4f27caa548e973c1b5cb607c3b9c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/logtest');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/logtest', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/logtest');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/logtest') !== 'b081c91eca8e4f27caa548e973c1b5cb607c3b9c') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/logtest') !== '56d77f3d2608ea24449c1d1bc9ec46f1dd277177') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/logtest');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/logtest');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/logtest')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/logtest', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/logtest') !== 'b081c91eca8e4f27caa548e973c1b5cb607c3b9c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/logtest');
		}
	}
}

	}

	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php') != 'fdf6bee970d5bbc33b9a424c25c60c71b23ae6a3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php');
	}

	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php') !== 'fdf6bee970d5bbc33b9a424c25c60c71b23ae6a3') {

			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplusLogger.class.php', $backup_name)) {

if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	writefile_23();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') != '8d1a3a3d4d8e6b78ee02b1398d988c6bdc58be94') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') !== '8d1a3a3d4d8e6b78ee02b1398d988c6bdc58be94') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') !== 'b220f50a2c0fb2f424f49e4fc92d9251d67429e3') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_23();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql') !== '8d1a3a3d4d8e6b78ee02b1398d988c6bdc58be94') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_mssql.sql');
		}
	}
}

	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('ZXJuYW1lYCkNCik7DQoNCkRST1AgVEFCTEUgSUYgRVhJU1RTIGBsb2dfb2JqZWN0YDsNCkNSRUFURSBUQUJMRSBgbG9nX29iamVjdGAgKA0KICBgaWRgIElOVEVHRVIgUFJJTUFSWSBLRVkgQVVUT0lOQ1JFTUVOVCwNCiAgYGxvZ19pZGAgSU5URUdFUiBOT1QgTlVM'));

}
if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql');
	writefile_26();
	if (!is_file('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql') != '8926022e4a6e43d8904e08b749580930b937cad3') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql') !== '8926022e4a6e43d8904e08b749580930b937cad3') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql') !== '2bb99f9712712897ed5dc30db5456dded51e0abd') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_26();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql') !== '8926022e4a6e43d8904e08b749580930b937cad3') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/sql/struct_sqlite.sql');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 288\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 288') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
